Two static helper methods, localRetentionMs() and localRetentionSize(), calculate the effective retention values based on whether remote log storage is enabled and configured.\\n\\nFor local segment file deletion, LocalLog.java (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/LocalLog.java) provides the deleteSegmentFiles() method which handles the physical deletion of segment files with optional async deletion support.\\n\\nFor remote log tiered storage, RemoteLogManager.java (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/server/log/remote/storage/RemoteLogManager.java) implements retention enforcement through its inner class RemoteLogRetentionHandler, which checks segment deletion conditions based on retention size (isSegmentBreachedBySize()), retention time (isSegmentBreachedByTime()), and log start offset. The manager builds retention data structures using buildRetentionTimeData() and buildRetentionSizeData() methods to determine which remote segments should be deleted.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
